flowchart TD
    Start([Start]) --> LoadFile[Load DATA_FILE]
    LoadFile --> InitCounter[Initialize Counter]
    InitCounter --> ForLoop{For each line in file}
    ForLoop --> ParseJSON[Parse JSON from line]
    ParseJSON --> ExtractKeys[Extract request keys]
    ExtractKeys --> RunEvent[Call run_event with params]
    RunEvent --> CheckResponse{Response has etaDate?}

    CheckResponse -->|Yes| CalcMetrics[Calculate ETA metrics]
    CalcMetrics --> CheckLate{Was delivery late?}

    UpdateCounters --> NextIter[Next iteration]
    NextIter --> ForLoop
    ForLoop -->|Done| CalcRates[Calculate false alarm rate and avg error]
    CalcRates --> PrintResults[Print results]

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[run_event] --> B[Create request_json]
    B --> C[Create Context with 5s timeout]
    C --> D[Call lambda_handler]
    D --> E{Exception?}
    E -->|Yes| F[Print traceback]
    E -->|No| G[Parse response]
    F --> H[Return response_json]
    G --> H
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Main as simulate_bad_alert_events
    participant File as DATA_FILE
    participant RunEvent as run_event
    participant Lambda as lambda_handler
    participant Counter as collections.Counter
    
    Main->>File: Open and read lines
    File-->>Main: Return lines
    Main->>Counter: Initialize counter
    loop For each event line
        Main->>Main: Parse JSON
        Main->>Main: Extract request keys
        Main->>RunEvent: Call with query params
        RunEvent->>Lambda: Call with request_json and context
        Lambda-->>RunEvent: Return response
        RunEvent-->>Main: Return response_json
        Main->>Main: Calculate ETA differences
        Main->>Main: Check if late/predicted late
        Main->>Counter: Update metrics
    end
    Main->>Main: Calculate false alarm rate
    Main->>Main: Calculate average error
    Main->>File: Write results to result.txt
```

### SVG

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> LoadingData
    LoadingData --> ProcessingEvent: File loaded
    ProcessingEvent --> MakingAPICall: Event parsed
    MakingAPICall --> AnalyzingResponse: API responds
    AnalyzingResponse --> CalculatingMetrics: ETA found
    AnalyzingResponse --> ProcessingEvent: No ETA, next event
    CalculatingMetrics --> UpdatingCounters: Metrics calculated
    UpdatingCounters --> ProcessingEvent: More events
    UpdatingCounters --> GeneratingResults: All events processed
    GeneratingResults --> WritingOutput: Results calculated
    WritingOutput --> [*]
```
